`0,~`~`--~`green~`value~J~`~`~`~`["b"]~`=~`0.88,~`~`--~`blue~`value~J~`~`~`~`["a"]~`=~`1,~`~`--~`alpha~`value~J}~J--------------------~J--~`How~`Doom~`works~`--~J--------------------~J~J--~`Doom~`is~`a~`dot,~`it~`ticks~`for~`damage~`at~`the~`end~`of~`it's~`duration.~`~J--~`Doom~`can~`partially~`tick~`if~`it's~`doesn't~`tick~`for~`it's~`full~`tickrate.~`~J--~`If~`doom~`is~`going~`to~`fall~`off~`before~`reaching~`it's~`full~`tick~`duration,~`the~`tick~`will~`happen~`at~`the~`end~`of~`Doom's~`duration~`unless~`doom~`is~`refreshed.~`Then~`the~`current~`tick~`will~`take~`how~`ever~`much~`more~`time~`it~`needs~`from~`the~`refresh~`to~`fully~`tick~J--~`Doom's~`pandemic~`window~`is~`based~`on~`your~`current~`haste~`(it's~`current~`tickrate)~J--~`Shard~`generation~`is~`based~`on~`how~`long~`doom~`was~`up~`for~`before~`it~`ticked~`vs~`it's~`tickrate.~`~J--~`Doom~`snapshots~`haste~`on~`cast,~`but~`the~`hasted~`interval~`is~`only~`calculated,~`from~`the~`next~`tick.~J~J-------------~J--~`Examples--~J-------------~J~J--~`Short~`->~`Long~`|~`(High~`Haste~`->~`Low~`Haste)~`--~J~J--~`Let's~`assume~`that~`you~`cast~`doom,~`with~`haste~`such~`that~`it's~`tickrate~`is~`10~`seconds.~`~J--~`Your~`haste~`when~`you~`casted~`the~`Doom,~`has~`now~`snapshotted~`it's~`tickrate~`(10~`seconds).~J--~`If~`your~`haste~`effects~`now~`fall~`off,~`such~`that~`Doom's~`tickrate~`is~`now~`20~`seconds~`(Doom's~`pandemic~`is~`now~`6~`seconds).~J--~`Assume~`that~`you~`now~`refresh~`doom~`at~`4~`seconds~`remaining,~`bringing~`it's~`duration~`up~`to~`24~`seconds.~J--~`Doom~`will~`then~`tick~`4~`seconds~`after~`the~`refresh~`at~`20~`seconds,~`for~`a~`full~`tick.~J--~`The~`next~`doom~`tick~`then~`starts,~`snapshotting~`the~`last~`refresh's~`haste~`as~`it's~`tickrate.~`~J~J--~`Long~`->~`Short~`|~`(Low~`Haste~`->~`High~`Haste)~`--~J~J--~`Let's~`say~`that~`you~`opened~`with~`Hand~`of~`Gul'dan~`(before~`your~`haste~`procs~`and~`Bloodlust).~`Applying~`a~`Doom~`with~`a~`tickrate~`of~`20~`seconds~`(snapshotting~`your~`haste).~J--~`Now~`you~`gain~`some~`haste,~`through~`the~`effects~`of~`Bloodlust~`and~`whispers.~`Doom's~`tickrate~`is~`brought~`down~`to~`10~`seconds.~J--~`While~`under~`the~`haste~`effects,~`you~`refresh~`doom~`at~`5~`seconds.~`Bringing~`the~`duration~`down~`to~`13~`seconds~`(10~`+~`10*0.3),~`because~`it's~`current~`pandemic~`is~`3~`seconds~J--~`You've~`now~`brought~`the~`duration~`of~`a~`Doom,~`with~`the~`tickrate~`of~`20~`seconds,~`down~`to~`13~`seconds.~J--~`You~`will~`get~`a~`tick~`at~`the~`end~`of~`dooms~`duration,~`that~`will~`deal~`65%~`damage~`(13/20)~`and~`have~`a~`65%~`change~`to~`generate~`a~`shard.~`~J~J-------------------------~J--~`Extended~`ticklength~`--~J-------------------------~J~J--~`Let's~`imagine~`a~`situation~`in~`which~`you~`refresh~`a~`short~`doom,~`with~`a~`long~`duration~`above~`it's~`pandemic~`threshold.~J--~`For~`simplicity~`we'll~`keep~`the~`ticks~`at~`10~`and~`20~`respectively.~J--~`You~`cast~`Doom~`to~`start~`the~`fight.~`Then~`refresh~`it~`with~`Hand~`of~`Gul'dan~`when~`it~`has~`9~`seconds~`remaining~`(1~`seconds~`after~`you~`applied~`it).~J--~`This~`brings~`the~`duration~`up~`to~`26~`seconds~`(20~`+~`0.3*20).~`~J--~`Doom~`will~`tick~`at~`17~`seconds~`remaining~`(9~`seconds~`after~`the~`refresh),~`snapshotting~`the~`next~`hasted~`interval~`with~`the~`last~`refreshed~`tickrate~`(20~`seconds)~J--~`Following~`the~`logic~`provided,~`Doom~`should~`partially~`tick~`at~`the~`end~`of~`it's~`duration~`for~`85%~`damage,~`and~`an~`85%~`chance~`to~`generate~`a~`shard.~J--~`Now's~`assume~`that~`you~`refresh~`Doom~`before~`it~`expires~`at~`3~`seconds~`remaining,~`pushing~`doom's~`duration~`to~`23~`seconds~`(20~`+~`3).~J--~`Doom~`now~`has~`enough~`time~`to~`make~`a~`full~`tick,~`so~`the~`nexttick~`will~`get~`pushed~`back~`from~`the~`time~`at~`which~`it~`would~`have~`expired~`to~`6~`seconds~`after~`the~`refresh~`(17~`seconds~`remaning)~`~J~J----------~J--~`Todo~`--~J----------~J--~`make~`a~`long~`term~`solution~`for~`cost~`reduction~`on~`spells~`from~`items~`and~`tier~J~J---------------------~J--~`Shard~`Cost~`Info~`--~J---------------------~JsoulShard_CostInfo~`=~`{~`--~`[spell]~`=~`{cost,~`dynamic~`cost,~`max~`cost,~`reduced~`cost~`item,~`amount~`reduced}~`~J~`~`~`~`--~`Affliction~`~J~`~`~`~`[GetSpellInfo(30108)]~`=~`{1},~`~`--~`Unstable~`Affliction~J~`~`~`~`[GetSpellInfo(27243)]~`=~`{1},~`~`--~`Seed~`of~`Corruption~J~`~`~`~`--~`Destruction~J~`~`~`~`[GetSpellInfo(116858)]~`=~`{2},~`~`--~`Chaos~`Bolt~J~`~`~`~`[GetSpellInfo(5740)]~`=~`{3},~`~`--~`Rain~`of~`Fire~J~`~`~`~`--~`Demonology~J~`~`~`~`[GetSpellInfo(105174)]~`=~`{1,~`true,~`4},~`~`--~`Hand~`of~`Gul'dan~J~`~`~`~`[GetSpellInfo(104316)]~`=~`{2,~`false,~`nil,~`aura_env.recurrentRitual,~`1},~`~`--~`Call~`Dreadstalkers~J~`~`~`~`--~`General~J~`~`~`~`[GetSpellInfo(18540)]~`=~`{1},~`~`--~`Summon~`Doomguard~J~`~`~`~`[GetSpellInfo(688)]~`=~`{1},~`~`--~`Summon~`Imp~J~`~`~`~`[GetSpellInfo(1122)]~`=~`{1},~`~`--~`Summon~`Infernal~J~`~`~`~`[GetSpellInfo(691)]~`=~`{1},~`~`--~`Summon~`Felhunter~J~`~`~`~`[GetSpellInfo(712)]~`=~`{1},~`~`--~`Summon~`Succubus~J~`~`~`~`[GetSpellInfo(697)]~`=~`{1},~`~`--~`Summon~`Voidwalker~J~`~`~`~`[GetSpellInfo(30146)]~`=~`{1}~`~`--~`Summon~`Felguard~J}~J--~`Calculate~`how~`many~`shards~`are~`going~`to~`be~`spent~JsoulShard_getPowerFromCast~`=~`function()~J~`~`~`~`local~`cast~`=~`UnitCastingInfo("player")~`or~`UnitChannelInfo("player")~`or~`nil~J~`~`~`~`if~`not~`cast~`then~J~`~`~`~`~`~`~`~`return~`0~J~`~`~`~`end~J~`~`~`~`local~`data~`=~`soulShard_CostInfo[cast]~`or~`nil~J~`~`~`~`~J~`~`~`~`if~`not~`data~`then~J~`~`~`~`~`~`~`~`return~`0~J~`~`~`~`end~J~`~`~`~`local~`power~`=~`data[1]~`or~`0~`~J~`~`~`~`if~`data[2]~`then~J~`~`~`~`~`~`~`~`power~`=~`UnitPower("player",~`~`Enum.PowerType.SoulShards,~`false)~J~`~`~`~`~`~`~`~`if~`power~`>=~`data[3]~`then~J~`~`~`~`~`~`~`~`~`~`~`~`power~`=~`data[3]~J~`~`~`~`~`~`~`~`end~J~`~`~`~`end~J~`~`~`~`if~`data[4]~`then~J~`~`~`~`~`~`~`~`power~`=~`power~`-~`data[5]~J~`~`~`~`end~J~`~`~`~`return~`power~Jend~J~J--~
